<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On March&nbsp;7, 2019, Plug Power Inc., a Delaware corporation (the &#147;Registrant&#148;), released its financial results for the quarter ended December&nbsp;31, 2018 and full year 2018 by posting its Fourth Quarter and Full Year 2018 Shareholder Letter on its website. The full text of the shareholder letter is attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 and is incorporated by reference in this Item 2.02.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information in this Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K (including the exhibits) is furnished pursuant to Item 2.02 and shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section.</font></p>

<body link=blue bgcolor="white" lang="EN-US">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="right" style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1<a name="Exhibit99_1_074848"></a></font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="720" height="128" src="g60651mm01i001.jpg"></font></p>
<p align="center" style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Plug Power Reports Breakthrough Fourth Quarter of 2018</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Positive adjusted EBITDA; over 75% revenue growth versus 4Q 2017</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="border:none;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="border:none;">Fourth quarter gross billings of $62.1 million versus $32.9 million gross billings in fourth quarter 2017. The Company in 2018 had total gross billings of $184.8 million, a 42% increase versus 2017.</font></p>
<p style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="border:none;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="border:none;">Positive adjusted EBITDA for fourth quarter 2018, the first in the Company&#146;s history</font></p>
<p style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="border:none;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="border:none;">GAAP loss per share of $0.08; adjusted loss per share of $0.07</font></p>
<p style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="border:none;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="border:none;">Delivered fuel cell systems to power over 1,900 zero emission electric vehicles</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Plug Power&#146;s record setting quarter is a result of technical leadership and continued new product deployment, coupled with constant attention to improving service. These focal points were key to delivering positive adjusted EBITDA for the first time in Company history. The organization successfully enhanced the reliability of our technology while serving a loyal customer base that allowed us to spend the year further cementing our position as the industry&#146;s global leader in hydrogen powered electric mobility.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="640" height="211" src="g60651mm01i002.jpg"></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Long-Term Success in Material Handling</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">In the fourth quarter of 2018, the Company sold over 1,900 GenDrive fuel cell units, dispensed 1.2 million tons of hydrogen into electric vehicles, built and commissioned three GenFuel hydrogen fueling stations, and delivered products to 15 different customers. These customers included Amazon, Walmart, Supervalu, Whole Foods and BMW.&#160; The breakthrough achievement of positive adjusted EBITDA in fourth quarter of 2018 is a direct result of the progress made by the Company on sales, market penetration, service improvement, and cost management.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="124" height="24" src="g60651mm01i003.jpg"></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">1<a name="PB_1_075238_455"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='1',FILE='C:\JMS\109929\19-6065-1\task9247310\6065-1-mm-01.htm',USER='109929',CD='Mar  7 08:19 2019' -->

<div style="page-break-before:always;"></div>
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Today, Plug Power has deployed over 25,000 GenDrive fuel cell units with some of the world&#146;s largest companies and built more than 80 GenFuel fueling stations. These Plug Power designed and constructed stations deliver over 16 tons of hydrogen daily to electric vehicles.&#160; These accomplishments have defined the benchmarks around the world for electric vehicle deployment and hydrogen fueling stations.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">In 2018, we emphasized our focus on building a profitable material handling business, a market quantified by currently having over 6 million forklift trucks in the field. These efforts continue in 2019 as we innovate more efficient and cost-reduced solutions to increase the ease and efficiency of using hydrogen fuel cell solutions in mobility applications &#151; such as leveraging the IoT (Internet of Things) to perform data/real time monitoring to provide seamless service to customers while improving the profitability of our business.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ProGen Engines: Changing the Way the World Moves</font></b></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="187" height="202" src="g60651mm01i004.jpg"></font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">KPMG&#146;s 2018 industry market study stated that hydrogen fuel cell vehicles (HFCV) have replaced battery powered electric vehicles (BEV) as the number one trend through 2025 (KPMG&#146;s 19th Global Automotive Executive Survey 2018). Plug Power&#146;s ProGen line of OEM hydrogen engines are designed specifically to capitalize on this strategic trend and position the Company for continued growth over the coming years.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">ProGen is a range of hydrogen fuel-cell engines, geared towards a variety of mobility and stationary applications. ProGen offers a modular and scalable architecture that makes it simple for customers to deploy in a wide variety of applications, including on-road vehicles (e.g. delivery vans), material handling, AGV&#146;s, ground support equipment, drones, and wireless 5G telecom gear.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">The electric vehicle (EV) use-case demands solutions that support high utilization and extended runtimes, require reliable performance in harsh environments, allow rapid fueling, and emit zero emissions. We&#146;ve already created the first commercially viable market for fuel cells in material handling, an industry with these same demands. Plug Power, through its ProGen engine offering, is leveraging our years of real-world experience to enable electric mobility through the power of hydrogen fuel cells.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">2<a name="PB_2_075316_4141"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\JMS\109929\19-6065-1\task9247310\6065-1-mm-01.htm',USER='109929',CD='Mar  7 08:19 2019' -->

<div style="page-break-before:always;"></div>
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ProGen Metal Stack Development</font></b></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Plug Power shipped a record 10,000 stacks to customers in 2018. During 2019, the Company is focused on continuing to lead the charge in both MEA and PEM fuel cell stack design and manufacturing.&#160; MEA capability was vertically integrated into Plug Power with the strategic technology acquisition of American Fuel Cell (AFC) in 2018.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Combining our MEA design expertise with high-tech production equipment, such as Kodak&#146;s digital high-speed coating technology, we&#146;ve been able to ramp up production, manufacturing more than 10,000 Plug Power MEAs to date, with plans to ramp to an annualized run rate of 400,000 in 2019. Not only are we thrilled with the speed and quality of production, Plug Power takes pride in bringing the production of a key technology product back to the United States. At the start of the fourth quarter of 2018, the Company began shipping production stacks to customers utilizing this in-house MEA technology. Based on numbers put forth in 2018 and our aggressive ramp in 2019, we expect Plug Power to be the largest US MEA supplier by year end.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Plug Power&#146;s proprietary MEA technology is a key component of the new ProGen metal stacks, the heart of our ProGen hydrogen engines.&#160; Our recently launched ProGen stack, based on metal plate technology, provides Plug Power with a competitive edge over other conventional graphite-based plate stack designs.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">This powerful combination produces a best-in-class automotive stack design for electric mobility applications. These stacks are two and a half times denser than our prior technology and offer a 25% cost reduction at volume.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">With the launch of this new ProGen stack, Plug Power continues its commitment to innovation and its goal of accelerating the adoption of zero emission hydrogen fuel cell electric vehicles (FCEVs).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="298" height="244" src="g60651mm01i005.jpg"></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fuel Cell Electric Vehicles for Fleet Applications</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">The world is going electric, and hydrogen fuel cells are ideal for commercial electric vehicle applications that demand high-asset utilization or extended range, such as delivery vans, taxis, buses, and municipal/government fleet vehicles. The value proposition for FCEVs includes 10x higher power density than traditional BEVs, greater vehicle range, fast fueling, and the ease of using a simple centralized fueling n infrastructure.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">3<a name="PB_3_075324_8627"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='3',FILE='C:\JMS\109929\19-6065-1\task9247310\6065-1-mm-01.htm',USER='109929',CD='Mar  7 08:19 2019' -->

<div style="page-break-before:always;"></div>
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Plug Power delivered the first ProGen-powered delivery van to FedEx at the start of 2018 &#151; today, the vehicle has covered over 14,000 miles delivering packages and has performed flawlessly.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Fuel cells bring significant value to this tethered vehicle market and on-road fleet vehicles are a key area of growth for our ProGen engine line. Turnkey, &#147;plug and play&#148; ProGen engines are designed to allow rapid integration into OEM vehicle platforms. In 2019, Plug Power expects to make further progress with a variety of EV partners across the globe.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="395" height="259" src="g60651mm01i006.jpg"></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Now, a review of our financial performance.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fourth Quarter Operational Performance and Financial Results</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Net revenue for the fourth quarter of 2018 was $59.8 million, versus net revenue of $31.1 million for fourth quarter of 2017.&#160; Included in our financial results is a $2.3 million provision for common stock warrants reported as a reduction of revenue in fourth quarter of 2018, versus a $1.8 million provision recorded in fourth quarter of 2017. As reported previously, these charges are associated with accounting for warrants stemming from our customer agreements with Amazon and Walmart.&#160; Future revenue reductions will occur over time until each of the customers reaches a cumulative $600 million of qualified purchases.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Key operating metrics for the fourth quarter of 2018 include:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="border:none;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="border:none;">Approximately 1,700 GenDrive units shipped in the quarter (1,900 recognized as revenue), versus 1,200 GenDrive units shipped in fourth quarter of 2017 (700 recognized as revenue).</font></p>
<p style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="border:none;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="border:none;">Three GenFuel sites sold in the quarter, versus zero for fourth quarter of 2017.</font></p>
<p style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="border:none;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="border:none;">Approximately 20,000 GenDrive units under service or PPA contract at December&nbsp;31, 2018, versus approximately 16,000 at December&nbsp;31, 2017.</font></p>
<p style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="border:none;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="border:none;">72 sites under fuel delivery contract at December&nbsp;31, 2018, versus 58 sites at December&nbsp;31, 2017.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">GAAP gross profit for the fourth quarter of 2018 was $4.5 million, compared to negative $0.7 million for the prior year.&#160; Adjusted gross profit for the fourth quarter of 2018 was $6.1 million, or</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">4<a name="PB_4_075334_7906"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\109929\19-6065-1\task9247310\6065-1-mm-01.htm',USER='109929',CD='Mar  7 08:19 2019' -->

<div style="page-break-before:always;"></div>
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">10% of net revenue.&#160;&#160; Adjusted gross profit excludes the interest component of operating leases associated with project financings.&#160; Adjusted gross profit for the fourth quarter of 2017 on a comparable basis was $0.8 million, or 3% of net revenue.&#160; The improvement in gross margins versus the prior year stems from ongoing volume leverage, product cost downs, and reliability investments in the service and fuel product lines.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">GAAP net loss attributable to common shareholders for the fourth quarter of 2018 was $16.9 million, or $0.08 loss per share.&#160; The GAAP net loss attributable to common shareholders in the fourth quarter of 2017 was $19.5 million, or $0.09 loss per share on a diluted basis.&#160; Adjusted loss per share in the fourth quarter 2018 was $0.07, which excludes certain one-time charges.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Net cash used by operating activities for the fourth quarter of 2018 was $16.0 million, compared to net cash provided of $21.1 million in 2017 (variation mainly due to working capital conversion timing).&#160; Adjusted EBITDA for the fourth quarter of 2018 was $0.5 million, compared to negative $7.6 million for the fourth quarter of 2017.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Plug Power has historically financed its Power Purchase Agreement deployments via operating and finance leases, and, as a result, the Company&#146;s financial results are significantly influenced by relevant lease accounting standards.&#160; As previously reported, the Company adopted a new lease accounting standard in the third quarter of 2018, effective January&nbsp;1, 2018.&#160; The most significant impact was the recognition of right of use assets and finance obligations for operating leases now reflected in the Consolidated Balance Sheets. The Company recorded the present value of its future minimum operating lease payments as a liability and recognized an amortizing asset for its &#147;right-of-use&#148;.&#160; Operating rent expense, included in cost of goods sold going forward, will include the interest component on the Company&#146;s operating lease liability and amortization of its right-of-use asset. In effect, this will align these operating leases more closely with how the Company accounts for finance leases.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Although it appears the level of expense for these operating leases will be consistent with the previous accounting standard, the future financial statement presentation driven from the new standard highlights the commonality that both operating and finance leases are fundamentally means to finance these deployments.&#160; Given there is and will continue to be an interest component within operating rent expense reported in GAAP cost of goods sold, Plug Power has excluded it when calculating adjusted gross profit; as is done for finance leases on a GAAP basis.&#160; Likewise, since leased asset depreciation and interest on finance leases have been excluded from adjusted EBITDA historically, Plug Power has excluded the similar amounts currently included as operating lease expense when calculating adjusted EBITDA.&#160; Both adjustments have been reflected in reported periods to separate financing from the ongoing traditional metrics used to measure true operational performance.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">5<a name="PB_5_075342_3736"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>

<div style="page-break-before:always;"></div>
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cash and Liquidity</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Operating cash flow used by operating activities for full year 2018 was $57.6 compared to $60.2 million for full year 2017.&#160; Overall the Company has recognized improvement in margin expansion and project financing programs with financial institutions that have been structured during the year.&#160; The Company anticipates these trends to continue improving its operating cash flow trends.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">As of December&nbsp;31, 2018, Plug Power had a total cash position of $110.2 million, including cash and cash equivalents of $38.6 million and restricted cash of $71.6 million.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Plug Power Inc.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">The architect of modern hydrogen and fuel cell technology, Plug Power is the innovator that has taken hydrogen and fuel cell technology from concept to commercialization. Plug Power has revolutionized the material handling industry with its full-service GenKey solution, which is designed to increase productivity, lower operating costs and reduce carbon footprints in a reliable, cost-effective way. The Company&#146;s GenKey solution couples together all the necessary elements to power, fuel and serve a customer. With proven hydrogen and fuel cell products, Plug Power replaces lead acid batteries to power electric industrial vehicles, such as the lift trucks customers use in their distribution centers.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;">Extending its reach into the on-road electric vehicle market, Plug Power&#146;s ProGen platform of modular fuel cell engines empowers OEMs and system integrators to rapidly adopt hydrogen fuel cell technology. ProGen engines are proven today, with thousands in service, supporting some of the most rugged operations in the world. Plug Power is the partner that customers trust to take their businesses into the future. www.plugpower.com.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="border:none;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="border:none;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note on Forward Looking Statements</font></b></p>

our ability to successfully expand internationally; our ability to improve system reliability for our GenDrive, GenSure and GenKey systems; competitive factors, such as price competition and competition from other traditional and alternative energy companies; <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Notes</font></u></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To supplement the Company&#146;s unaudited financial data presented on a generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) basis, management has used adjusted gross profit, adjusted EBITDA and adjusted diluted net loss per share which are non-GAAP measures.&#160; These non-GAAP measures are among the indicators management uses as a basis for evaluating the Company&#146;s financial performance as well as for forecasting future periods.&#160; Management establishes performance targets, annual budgets and makes operating decisions based in part upon these metrics. Accordingly, disclosure of these non-GAAP measures provides investors with the same information that management uses to understand the Company&#146;s economic performance year over year. In addition, investors have historically requested and the Company has historically reported these non-GAAP financial measures as a means of providing consistent and comparable information with past reports of financial results. The presentation of this additional information is not meant to be considered in isolation or as a substitute for net income or other measures prepared in accordance with GAAP.&#160; Adjusted gross profit, adjusted EBITDA and adjusted diluted net loss per share are not measures of our liquidity or financial performance under GAAP and should not be considered as an alternative to net income or any other performance measure derived in accordance with GAAP, or as an alternative to cash flows from operating activities as a measure of our liquidity. While management believes that the non-GAAP financial measures provide useful supplemental information to investors, there are limitations associated with the use of these measures.&#160; The measures are not prepared in accordance with GAAP and may not be directly comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies due to potential differences in the exact method of calculation.&#160; The Company&#146;s non-GAAP financial measures are not meant to be considered in isolation or as a substitute for comparable GAAP financial measures, and should be read only in conjunction with the Company&#146;s consolidated financial statements prepared in accordance with GAAP.</font></p>
